## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-868">Erros de inicialização do aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-868">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-869">No Visual Studio, um projeto do ASP.NET Core usa por padrão a hospedagem do [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante a depuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-869">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-870">Uma *falha de processo 502.5* que ocorre quando a depuração local pode ser diagnosticada usando o conselho neste tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-870">A *502.5 Process Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-871">403.14 Proibido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-871">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-872">O aplicativo não consegue iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-872">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-873">O seguinte erro está registrado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-873">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-874">O erro geralmente é causado por uma implantação quebrada no sistema de hospedagem, que inclui qualquer um dos seguintes cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-874">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-875">O aplicativo é implantado na pasta errada no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-875">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-876">O processo de implantação falhou em mover todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo para a pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-876">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-877">O arquivo *Web.config* está ausente da implantação, ou o conteúdo do arquivo *Web.config* está malformado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-877">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-878">Execute as seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-878">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-879">Exclua todos os arquivos e pastas da pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-879">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-880">Reimplante o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do aplicativo para o sistema de hospedagem usando seu método normal de implantação, como Visual Studio, PowerShell ou implantação manual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-880">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-881">Confirme se o arquivo *Web.config* está presente na implantação e que seu conteúdo está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-881">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-882">Ao hospedar no Azure App Service, confirme `D:\home\site\wwwroot` se o aplicativo está implantado na pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-882">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-883">Quando o aplicativo estiver hospedado pelo IIS, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado no **caminho físico** do IIS mostrado nas **Configurações Básicas**do **IIS Manager**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-883">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-884">Confirme se todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo foram implantados comparando a implantação no sistema de hospedagem com o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-884">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-885">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>de um aplicativo publicado ASP.NET Core, consulte .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-885">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-886">Para obter mais informações sobre o <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>arquivo *web.config,* consulte .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-886">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-887">500 Erro Interno do Servidor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-887">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-888">O aplicativo é iniciado, mas um erro impede o servidor de atender à solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-888">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-889">Esse erro ocorre no código do aplicativo durante a inicialização ou durante a criação de uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-889">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-890">A resposta poderá não conter nenhum conteúdo, ou a resposta poderá ser exibida como um *500 – Erro Interno do Servidor* no navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-890">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-891">O Log de Eventos do Aplicativo geralmente indica que o aplicativo iniciou normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-891">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-892">Da perspectiva do servidor, isso está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-892">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-893">O aplicativo foi iniciado, mas não é capaz de gerar uma resposta válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-893">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-894">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no servidor ou habilite o log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core para solucionar o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-894">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-895">502.5 Falha de processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-895">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-896">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-896">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-897">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-897">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-898">O [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o processo de trabalho, mas falhar ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-898">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-899">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-899">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-900">Uma condição de falha comum é o aplicativo configurado incorretamente, direcionado a uma versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-900">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-901">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-901">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-902">A *estrutura compartilhada* é o conjunto de assemblies (arquivos *. dll*) instalado no computador e referenciado por um metapacote como `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-902">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-903">A referência do metapacote pode especificar a versão mínima necessária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-903">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-904">Saiba mais em [A estrutura compartilhada](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-904">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-905">A página do erro *502.5 – Falha no Processo* é retornada quando um erro de configuração de hospedagem ou do aplicativo faz com que o processo de trabalho falhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-905">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-906">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-906">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-907">O aplicativo falhou ao ser iniciado porque o assembly do aplicativo (*.dll*) não pôde ser carregado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-907">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-908">Esse erro ocorre quando há uma incompatibilidade de número de bits entre o aplicativo publicado e o processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-908">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-909">Confirme se a configuração de 32 bits do pool de aplicativos está correta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-909">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-910">Selecione o pool de aplicativos no **Pools de Aplicativos** do Gerenciador do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-910">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-911">Selecione **Configurações Avançadas** em **Editar Pool de Aplicativos** no painel **Ações**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-911">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-912">Defina **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-912">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-913">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86), defina o valor como `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-913">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-914">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64), defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-914">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-915">Confirme se não há um `<Platform>` conflito entre uma propriedade MSBuild no arquivo do projeto e a bitividade publicada do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-915">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-916">Redefinição de conexão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-916">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-917">Se um erro ocorrer após os cabeçalhos serem enviados, será tarde demais para o servidor enviar um **500 – Erro Interno do Servidor** no caso de um erro ocorrer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-917">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-918">Isso geralmente acontece quando ocorre um erro durante a serialização de objetos complexos para uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-918">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-919">Esse tipo de erro é exibida como um erro de *redefinição de conexão* no cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-919">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-920">O [Log de aplicativo](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pode ajudar a solucionar esses tipos de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-920">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-921">Limites de inicialização padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-921">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-922">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) é configurado com uma *inicialização padrãoTimeLimit* de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-922">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-923">Quando deixado no valor padrão, um aplicativo pode levar até dois minutos para iniciar antes que uma falha do processo seja registrada em log pelo módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-923">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-924">Para obter informações sobre como configurar o módulo, veja [Atributos do elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-924">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-925">Solução de problemas no Serviço de Aplicativos Do Azure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-925">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-926">Registro de eventos de aplicativos (serviço de aplicativos do Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-926">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-927">Para acessar o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo, use a folha **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** no portal do Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-927">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-928">No portal do Azure, abra o aplicativo nos **Serviços de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-928">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-929">Selecione **Diagnóstico e solução de problemas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-929">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-930">Selecione o título **Ferramentas de Diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-930">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-931">Em **Ferramentas de Suporte**, selecione o botão **Eventos do Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-931">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-932">Examine o erro mais recente fornecido pela entrada *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* na coluna **Origem**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-932">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-933">Uma alternativa ao uso da folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** é examinar o arquivo de Log de Eventos do Aplicativo diretamente usando o [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-933">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-934">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-934">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-935">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-935">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-936">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-936">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-937">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-937">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-938">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-938">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-939">Selecione o ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-939">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-940">Examine o log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-940">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-941">Role até o final do log para ver os eventos mais recentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-941">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-942">Execute o aplicativo no console do Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-942">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-943">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-943">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-944">Você pode executar o aplicativo no Console de Execução Remota do [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) para descobrir o erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-944">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-945">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-945">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-946">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-946">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-947">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-947">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-948">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-948">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-949">Testar um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-949">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-950">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-950">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-951">Execute o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-951">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-952">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-952">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-953">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-953">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-954">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-954">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-955">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-955">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-956">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-956">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-957">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-957">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-958">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-958">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-959">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-959">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-960">Testar um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-960">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-961">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-961">**Current release**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-962">Se o aplicativo for uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) de 64 bits (x64):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-962">If the app is a 64-bit (x64) [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\Program Files\dotnet`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-963">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-963">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-964">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-964">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-965">Execute o aplicativo: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-965">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-966">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-966">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-967">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-967">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-968">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-968">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-969">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-969">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-970">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-970">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-971">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-971">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-972">ASP.NET registro de stdout do Módulo Central (Serviço de Aplicativos Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-972">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-973">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-973">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-974">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-974">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-975">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-975">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-976">Em **SELECIONAR CATEGORIA DE PROBLEMA**, selecione o botão **Aplicativo Web Inoperante**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-976">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-977">Em **Soluções Sugeridas** > **Habilitar o Redirecionamento de Log de Stdout**, selecione o botão para **Abrir o Console do Kudu para editar o Web.Config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-977">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-978">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-978">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-979">Role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-979">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-980">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-980">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-981">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-981">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-982">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-982">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-983">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-983">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-984">Volte para o portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-984">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-985">Selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-985">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-986">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-986">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-987">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-987">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-988">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-988">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-989">Abra a pasta **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-989">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-990">Inspecione a coluna **Modificado em** e selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o log de stdout com a data da última modificação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-990">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-991">Quando o arquivo de log é aberto, o erro é exibido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-991">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-992">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-992">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-993">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, retorne para o caminho **site** > **wwwroot** para revelar o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-993">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-994">Abra o arquivo **web.config** novamente, selecionando o ícone de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-994">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-995">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-995">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-996">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-996">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-997">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-997">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-998">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-998">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-999">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-999">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1000">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1000">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1001">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1001">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1002">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1002">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1003">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (Serviço de Aplicativos Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1003">Slow or hanging app (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1004">Para saber mais sobre quando um aplicativo responde lentamente ou trava em uma solicitação, confira os seguintes artigos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1004">When an app responds slowly or hangs on a request, see the following articles:</span></span>

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1007">Folhas de monitoramento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1007">Monitoring blades</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1008">As folhas de monitoramento fornecem uma experiência alternativa de solução de problemas para os métodos descritos anteriormente no tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1008">Monitoring blades provide an alternative troubleshooting experience to the methods described earlier in the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1009">Essas folhas podem ser usadas para diagnosticar erros da série 500.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1009">These blades can be used to diagnose 500-series errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1010">Verifique se as Extensões do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1010">Confirm that the ASP.NET Core Extensions are installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1011">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, instale-as manualmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1011">If the extensions aren't installed, install them manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1014">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, selecione o botão **Adicionar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1014">If the extensions aren't installed, select the **Add** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1015">Escolha as **Extensões do ASP.NET Core** da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1015">Choose the **ASP.NET Core Extensions** from the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1016">Selecione **OK** para aceitar os termos legais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1016">Select **OK** to accept the legal terms.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1017">Selecione **OK** na folha **Adicionar extensão**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1017">Select **OK** on the **Add extension** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1018">Uma mensagem pop-up informativa indica quando as extensões são instaladas com êxito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1018">An informational pop-up message indicates when the extensions are successfully installed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1019">Se o registro em log de stdout não estiver habilitado, siga estas etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1019">If stdout logging isn't enabled, follow these steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1020">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1020">In the Azure portal, select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1021">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1021">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1022">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1022">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1023">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1023">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1024">Abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot** e role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1024">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** and scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1025">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1025">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1026">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1026">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1027">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1027">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1028">Prossiga para ativar o log de diagnóstico:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1028">Proceed to activate diagnostic logging:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1029">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Logs de diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1029">In the Azure portal, select the **Diagnostics logs** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1030">Selecione a opção **Ligado** para **Log de Aplicativo (Sistema de arquivos)** e **Mensagens de erro detalhadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1030">Select the **On** switch for **Application Logging (Filesystem)** and **Detailed error messages**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1031">Selecione o botão **Salvar** na parte superior da folha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1031">Select the **Save** button at the top of the blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1032">Para incluir o rastreamento de solicitação com falha, também conhecido como FREB (Buffer de Evento de Solicitação com Falha), selecione a opção **Ligado** para o **Rastreamento de solicitação com falha**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1032">To include failed request tracing, also known as Failed Request Event Buffering (FREB) logging, select the **On** switch for **Failed request tracing**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1034">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1034">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1035">Dentro dos dados de fluxo de log, a causa do erro é indicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1035">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1036">Sempre desabilite o registro em log de stdout após concluir a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1036">Be sure to disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1037">Para exibir os logs de rastreamento de solicitação com falha (logs FREB):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1037">To view the failed request tracing logs (FREB logs):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1038">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1038">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1039">Selecione **Logs de Rastreamento de Solicitação com Falha** da área **FERRAMENTAS DE SUPORTE** da barra lateral.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1039">Select **Failed Request Tracing Logs** from the **SUPPORT TOOLS** area of the sidebar.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1040">Confira a [seção de Rastreamentos de solicitação com falha no tópico Habilitar o log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e as [Perguntas frequentes do desempenho do aplicativo para Aplicativos Web no Azure: como ativar o rastreamento de solicitação com falha?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1040">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1041">Para obter mais informações, veja [Habilitar log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1041">For more information, see [Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1042">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1042">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1043">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1043">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1044">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1044">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1045">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1045">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1046">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1046">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1047">Registro de eventos de aplicativos (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1047">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1048">Acesse o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1048">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1049">Abra o menu Iniciar, procure o *Visualizador de Eventos*e selecione o aplicativo **Visualizador de Eventos.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1049">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1050">No **Visualizador de Eventos**, abra o nó **Logs do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1050">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1051">Selecione **Aplicativo** para abrir o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1051">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1052">Procure erros associados ao aplicativo com falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1052">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1053">Os erros têm um valor *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS* ou *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS Express* na coluna *Origem*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1053">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1054">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1054">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1055">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1055">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1056">Você pode encontrar a causa de alguns erros ao executar o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1056">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1057">Implantação dependente de estrutura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1057">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1058">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1058">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1059">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o aplicativo, executando o assembly do aplicativo com *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1059">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1060">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1060">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1061">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1061">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1062">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1062">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1063">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1063">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1064">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1064">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1065">Implantação autocontida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1065">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1066">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1066">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1067">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o arquivo executável do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1067">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1068">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1068">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1069">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1069">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1070">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1070">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1071">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1071">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1072">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1072">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1073">ASP.NET registro de stdout do Módulo Central (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1073">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1074">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1074">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1075">Navegue até a pasta de implantação do site no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1075">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1076">Se a pasta *logs* não estiver presente, crie-a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1076">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1077">Para obter instruções sobre como habilitar o MSBuild para criar a pasta *logs* na implantação automaticamente, veja o tópico [Estrutura de diretórios](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1077">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1078">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1078">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1079">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para apontar para a pasta *logs* (por exemplo, `.\logs\stdout`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1079">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1080">`stdout` no caminho é o prefixo do nome do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1080">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1081">Uma extensão de arquivo, uma ID do processo e um carimbo de data/hora são adicionados automaticamente quando o log é criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1081">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1082">Usando `stdout` como o prefixo do nome do arquivo, um arquivo de log típico é nomeado *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1082">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1083">Verifique se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação para a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1083">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1084">Salve o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1084">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1085">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1085">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1086">Navegue até a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1086">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1087">Localize e abra o log de stdout mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1087">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1088">Estude o log em busca de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1088">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1089">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1089">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1090">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1090">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1091">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1091">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1092">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1092">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1093">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1093">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1094">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1094">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1095">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1095">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1096">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1096">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1097">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1097">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1098">Habilitar a página de exceção do desenvolvedor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1098">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1099">A  [variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` pode ser adicionada ao web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) para executar o aplicativo no ambiente de desenvolvimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1099">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1100">Desde que o ambiente não seja substituído na inicialização do aplicativo por `UseEnvironment` no compilador do host, definir a variável de ambiente permite que a [Página de Exceções do Desenvolvedor](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) apareça quando o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1100">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1101">Configurar a variável de ambiente para `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` só é recomendado para servidores de preparo e de teste que não estejam expostos à Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1101">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1102">Remova a variável de ambiente do arquivo *web.config* após a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1102">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1103">Para obter informações sobre como definir variáveis de ambiente no *web.config*, confira [Elemento filho environmentVariables de aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1103">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1104">Obter dados de um aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1104">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1105">Se um aplicativo for capaz de responder às solicitações, obtenha as solicitações, conexão e dados adicionais do aplicativo que usar o middleware embutido de terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1105">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1106">Para saber mais e obter um código de exemplo, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1106">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1107">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1107">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1108">Um *crash dump* é um instantâneo da memória do sistema e pode ajudar a determinar a causa de uma falha de aplicativo, falha de inicialização ou aplicativo lento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1108">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1109">O aplicativo falha ou encontra uma exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1109">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1110">Obter e analisar um despejo de memória do [WER (Relatório de Erros do Windows)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1110">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1111">Crie uma pasta para armazenar os arquivos de despejo de memória em `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1111">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1112">O pool de aplicativos deve ter acesso para gravação à pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1112">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1113">Execute o [script EnableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1113">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1114">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1114">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1115">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1115">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1116">Execute o aplicativo sob as condições que causam a falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1116">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1117">Após a falha, execute o [script DisableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1117">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1118">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1118">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1119">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1119">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1120">Depois que um aplicativo falhar e a coleta de despejo de memória for concluída, o aplicativo terá permissão para encerrar normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1120">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1121">O script do PowerShell configura o WER para coletar até cinco despejos de memória por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1121">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1122">Os despejos de memória podem usar uma grande quantidade de espaço em disco (até vários gigabytes cada).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1122">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1123">O aplicativo trava, falha durante a inicialização ou executa normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1123">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1124">Quando um aplicativo *é travado* (pára de responder, mas não falha), falha durante a inicialização ou é executado normalmente, consulte [Arquivos de despejo do modo de usuário: Escolhendo a melhor ferramenta](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) para selecionar uma ferramenta apropriada para produzir o dump.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1124">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1125">Analisar o despejo de memória</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1125">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1126">Um despejo de memória pode ser analisado usando várias abordagens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1126">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1127">Para obter mais informações, confira [Analisando um arquivo de despejo de memória do modo de usuário](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1127">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1128">Limpar caches de pacotes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1128">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1129">Um aplicativo em funcionamento pode falhar imediatamente após atualizar o .NET Core SDK na máquina de desenvolvimento ou alterar as versões do pacote dentro do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1129">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1130">Em alguns casos, pacotes incoerentes podem interromper um aplicativo ao executar atualizações principais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1130">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1131">A maioria desses problemas pode ser corrigida seguindo estas instruções:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1131">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1132">Exclua as pastas *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1132">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1133">Limpe os caches do pacote executando [os locais dotnet nuget tudo -- limpar](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) de um shell de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1133">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1134">A limpeza de caches de pacotes também pode ser realizada `nuget locals all -clear`com a ferramenta [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e executando o comando .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1134">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1135">*nuget.exe* não é uma instalação fornecida com o sistema operacional Windows Desktop e devem ser obtidos separadamente do [site do NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1135">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1136">Restaure e recompile o projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1136">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="89b7f-1137">Exclua todos os arquivos da pasta de implantação no servidor antes de reimplantar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="89b7f-1137">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>
